`product_i18n` `default_locale_i18n` ON (product.ID=default_locale_i18n.ID AND `default_locale_i18n`.LOCALE = 'fr_FR') LEFT JOIN `product_i18n` `requested_locale_i18n` ON (product.ID=requested_locale_i18n.ID AND `requested_locale_i18n`.LOCALE = 'fr_FR') INNER JOIN `product_category` `CategorySelect` ON (product.ID=CategorySelect.PRODUCT_ID) LEFT JOIN `sale_product` = 1) WHERE ((NOT ISNULL(`requested_locale_i18n`.ID) OR NOT ISNULL(`default_locale_i18n`.ID)) AND `pse`.PROMO=1) AND CategorySelect.DEFAULT_CATEGORY=1 AND product.VISIBLE=1 GROUP BY product.ID ORDER BY
